(\n\t\"bytes\"\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"embed\"\n\t\"encoding/json\"\n\t\"html/template\"\n\t\"io/fs\"\n\t\"log\"\n\t\"net/http\"\n\t\"strconv\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\t\"time\"\n\n\t\"homelab-dashboard/internal/config\"\n\t\"homelab-dashboard/internal/dashboard\"\n)\n\n//go:embed templates/*.gohtml static/*\nvar assets embed.FS\n\ntype dashboardService interface {\n\tHub(context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel\n\tSecurity(context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel\n\tAnomalies(context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel\n\tForecast(context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel\n}\n\ntype Server struct {\n\tcfg       config.Config\n\tservice dashboardService) *Server {\n\tfuncs := template.FuncMap{\n\t\t\"ago\": func(value time.Time) string {\n\t\t\tif value.IsZero() {\n\t\t\t\treturn \"n/a\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdiff := time.Since(value).Round(time.Minute)\n\t\t\tif diff < time.Minute {\n\t\t\t\treturn \"just now\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn diff.String() + \" ago\"\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"ts\": func(value time.Time) string {\n\t\t\tif value.IsZero() {\n\t\t\t\treturn \"\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn value.UTC().Format(time.RFC3339)\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"meterWidth\": func(value float64) string {\n\t\t\tif value < 0 {\n\t\t\t\tvalue = 0\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif value > 100 {\n\t\t\t\tvalue = 100\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn strings.TrimSpace(strings.TrimRight(strings.TrimRight(\n\t\t\t\tstrconv.FormatFloat(value, 'f', 1, 64), \"0\"), \".\")) + \"%\"\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"anomalyIcon\": func(severity string) string {\n\t\t\tswitch severity {\n\t\t\tcase \"critical\":\n\t\t\t\treturn \"error\"\n\t\t\tcase \"warning\":\n\t\t\t\treturn \"warning\"\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\treturn \"commit\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"timelineIcon\": func(label string) string {\n\t\t\tswitch strings.ToLower(strings.TrimSpace(label)) {\n\t\t\tcase \"compute\":\n\t\t\t\treturn \"memory\"\n\t\t\tcase \"network\":\n\t\t\t\treturn \"route\"\n\t\t\tcase \"storage\":\n\t\t\t\treturn \"database\"\n\t\t\tcase \"operators\":\n\t\t\t\treturn \"settings_suggest\"\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\treturn \"monitoring\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\n\ttmpl := template.Must(template.New(\"page.gohtml\").Funcs(funcs).ParseFS(assets, \"templates/*.gohtml\"))\n\tstaticRoot := mustSubFS(assets, \"static\")\n\n\treturn &Server{\n\t\tcfg:       cfg,\n\t\tservice:   service,\n\t\ttemplates: tmpl,\n\t\tstaticFS:  http.FileServer(http.FS(staticRoot)),\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) Routes() http.Handler {\n\tmux := http.NewServeMux()\n\n\tmux.Handle(\"/static/\", http.StripPrefix(\"/static/\", s.staticFS))\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/healthz\", func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\t_, _ = w.Write([]byte(\"ok\"))\n\t})\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/\", s.wrap(func(ctx context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel {\n\t\treturn s.service.Hub(ctx)\n\t}))\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/security\", s.wrap(func(ctx context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel {\n\t\treturn s.service.Security(ctx)\n\t}))\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/anomalies\", s.wrap(func(ctx context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel {\n\t\treturn s.service.Anomalies(ctx)\n\t}))\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/forecasting\", s.wrap(func(ctx context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel {\n\t\treturn s.service.Forecast(ctx)\n\t}))\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/api/view/hub\", s.apiWrap(func(ctx context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel {\n\t\treturn s.service.Hub(ctx)\n\t}))\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/api/view/security\", s.apiWrap(func(ctx context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel {\n\t\treturn s.service.Security(ctx)\n\t}))\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/api/view/anomalies\", s.apiWrap(func(ctx context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel {\n\t\treturn s.service.Anomalies(ctx)\n\t}))\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/api/view/forecasting\", s.apiWrap(func(ctx context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel {\n\t\treturn s.service.Forecast(ctx)\n\t}))\n\n\treturn mux\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) wrap(load func(context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tif r.URL.Path != \"/\" && r.URL.Path != \"/security\" && r.URL.Path != \"/anomalies\" && r.URL.Path != \"/forecasting\" {\n\t\t\thttp.NotFound(w, r)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), s.cfg.PrometheusTimeout)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tmodel := load(ctx)\n\t\tbodyHTML, err := s.renderBody(model)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"content render failed: %v\", err)\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"content render failed\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tview := pageView{\n\t\t\tViewModel: model,\n\t\t\tBodyHTML:  template.HTML(bodyHTML),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif err := s.templates.ExecuteTemplate(w, \"page\", view); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"template render failed: %v\", err)\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"template render failed\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) apiWrap(load func(context.Context) dashboard.ViewModel) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), s.cfg.PrometheusTimeout)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tmodel := load(ctx)\n\t\theaderHTML, err := s.renderPartial(\"topbar_meta\", model)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"header partial render failed: %v\", err)\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"header render failed\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbodyHTML, err := s.renderBody(model)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"content partial render failed: %v\", err)\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"content render failed\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tpayload := struct {\n\t\t\tHeaderHTML string `json:\"header_html\"`\n\t\t\tBodyHTML   string `json:\"body_html\"`\n\t\t}{\n\t\t\tHeaderHTML: headerHTML,\n\t\t\tBodyHTML:   bodyHTML,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tif err := json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(payload); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"json encode failed: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) renderBody(model dashboard.ViewModel) (string, error) {\n\treturn s.renderPartial(bodyTemplateName(model.Screen), model)\n}\n\nfunc (s *Server) renderPartial(name string, model dashboard.ViewModel) (string, error) {\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\tif err := s.templates.ExecuteTemplate(&buf, name, model); err != nil {\n\t\treturn \"\", err\n\t}\n\treturn buf.String(), nil\n}\n\nfunc bodyTemplateName(screen string) string {\n\tswitch screen {\n\tcase \"hub\":\n\t\treturn \"hub_body\"\n\tcase \"security\":\n\t\treturn \"security_body\"\n\tcase \"anomalies\":\n\t\treturn \"anomalies_body\"\n\tcase \"forecasting\":\n\t\treturn \"forecasting_body\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"hub_body\"\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc mustSubFS(root fs.FS, path string) fs.FS {\n\tsub, err := fs.Sub(root, path)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tpanic(err)\n\t}\n\treturn sub\n}\n\n---\npackage main\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"log\"\n\t\"net/http\"\n\t\"os\"\n\t\"os/signal\"\n\t\"syscall\"\n\t\"time\"\n\n\t\"homelab-dashboard/internal/buildinfo\"\n\t\"homelab-dashboard/internal/config\"\n\t\"homelab-dashboard/internal/dashboard\"\n\t\"homelab-dashboard/internal/kube\"\n\t\"homelab-dashboard/internal/prom\"\n\t\"homelab-dashboard/internal/web\"\n)\n\nfunc main() {\n\tcfg := config.Load()\n\n\tpromClient := prom.NewClient(cfg.PrometheusURL, cfg.PrometheusTimeout)\n\tkubeClient, kubeErr := kube.NewClient(cfg.KubeconfigPath)\n\tif kubeErr != nil {\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"kubernetes client disabled: %v\", kubeErr)\n\t}\n\n\tservice := dashboard.NewService(cfg, promClient, kubeClient)\n\thandler := web.NewServer(cfg, service)\n\n\tsrv := &http.Server{\n\t\tAddr:              \":\" + cfg.Port,\n\t\tHandler:           handler.Routes(),\n\t\tReadHeaderTimeout: 5 * time.Second,\n\t}\n\n\tctx, stop := signal.NotifyContext(context.Background(), os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)\n\tdefer stop()\n\n\tgo func() {\n\t\t<-ctx.Done()\n\n\t\tshutdownCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 10*time.Second)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t\tif err := srv.Shutdown(shutdownCtx); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"server shutdown failed: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tlog.Printf(\"starting %s version=%s commit=%s on :%s\", cfg.AppName, buildinfo.Version, buildinfo.Commit, cfg.Port)\n\tif err := srv.ListenAndServe(); err != nil && err != http.ErrServerClosed {\n\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"server len(raw))\n\t}\n\n\ttsFloat, ok := raw[0].(float64)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn time.Time{}, 0, fmt.Errorf(\"timestamp is %T\", raw[0])\n\t}\n\n\tvalueString, ok := raw[1].(string)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn time.Time{}, 0, fmt.Errorf(\"value is %T\", raw[1])\n\t}\n\n\tvalue, err := strconv.ParseFloat(valueString, 64)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tif strings.EqualFold(valueString, \"nan\") {\n\t\t\tvalue = math.NaN()\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\treturn time.Time{}, 0, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tseconds := int64(tsFloat)\n\tnanos := int64((tsFloat - float64(seconds)) * float64(time.Second))\n\treturn (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"encoding/json\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"io\"\n\t\"math\"\n\t\"net/http\"\n\t\"net/url\"\n\t\"strconv\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\t\"time\"\n)\n\ntype Client struct {\n\tbaseURL    string\n\thttpClient *http.Client\n}\n\ntype Sample struct {\n\tMetric    map[string]string\n\tTimestamp time.Time\n\tValue     float64\n}\n\ntype RangeSeries struct {\n\tMetric map[string]string\n\tPoints []Point\n}\n\ntype Point struct {\n\tTimestamp time.Time\n\tValue     float64\n}\n\nfunc NewClient(baseURL string, timeout time.Duration) *Client {\n\treturn &Client{\n\t\tbaseURL: strings.TrimRight(baseURL, \"/\"),\n\t\thttpClient: &http.Client{\n\t\t\tTimeout: timeout,\n\t\t},\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (c *Client) Query(ctx context.Context, query string) ([]Sample, error) {\n\tresponse := promResponse{}\n\tif err := c.do(ctx, \"/api/v1/query\", url.Values{\"query\": []string{query}}, &response); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tsamples := make([]Sample, 0, len(response.Data.Result))\n\tfor _, raw := range response.Data.Result {\n\t\ttimestamp, value, err := parseValuePair(raw.Value)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"parse sample %q: %w\", query, err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tsamples = append(samples, Sample{\n\t\t\tMetric:    raw.Metric,\n\t\t\tTimestamp: timestamp,\n\t\t\tValue:     value,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\treturn samples, nil\n}\n\nfunc (c *Client) QueryRange(ctx context.Context, query string, start, end time.Time, step time.Duration) ([]RangeSeries, error) {\n\tresponse := promRangeResponse{}\n\tvalues := url.Values{\n\t\t\"query\": []string{query},\n\t\t\"start\": []string{strconv.FormatInt(start.Unix(), 10)},\n\t\t\"end\":   []string{strconv.FormatInt(end.Unix(), 10)},\n\t\t\"step\":  []string{strconv.FormatFloat(step.Seconds(), 'f', -1, 64)},\n\t}\n\n\tif err := c.do(ctx, \"/api/v1/query_range\", values, &response); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tseries := make([]RangeSeries, 0, len(response.Data.Result))\n\tfor _, raw := range response.Data.Result {\n\t\tpoints := make([]Point, 0, len(raw.Values))\n\t\tfor _, pair := range raw.Values {\n\t\t\ttimestamp, value, err := parseValuePair(pair)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"parse range sample %q: %w\", query, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tpoints = append(points, Point{Timestamp: timestamp, Value: value})\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tseries = append(series, RangeSeries{\n\t\t\tMetric: raw.Metric,\n\t\t\tPoints: points,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\treturn series, nil\n}\n\nfunc (c *Client) Scalar(ctx context.Context, query string) (float64, error) {\n\tsamples, err := c.Query(ctx, query)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn 0, err\n\t}\n\n\tif len(samples) == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0, nil\n\t}\n\n\treturn samples[0].Value, nil\n}\n\nfunc (c *Client) do(ctx context.Context, path string, values url.Values, target any) error {\n\tendpoint, err := url.Parse(c.baseURL + path)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"parse endpoint: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tendpoint.RawQuery = values.Encode()\n\n\treq, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, endpoint.String(), nil)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"build request: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tresp, err := c.httpClient.Do(req)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"prometheus request failed: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tdefer resp.Body.Close()\n\n\tif resp.StatusCode >= http.StatusBadRequest {\n\t\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(io.LimitReader(resp.Body, 4096))\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"prometheus returned %s: %s\", resp.Status, strings.TrimSpace(string(body)))\n\t}\n\n\tif err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(target); err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"decode response: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc parseValuePair(raw []any) (time.Time, float64, error) {\n\tif len(raw) != 2 {\n\t\treturn time.Time{}, 0, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected pair length %d\", len(raw))\n\t}\n\n\ttsFloat, ok := raw[0].(float64)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn time.Time{}, 0, fmt.Errorf(\"timestamp is %T\", raw[0])\n\t}\n\n\tvalueString, ok := raw[1].(string)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn time.Time{}, 0, fmt.Errorf(\"value is %T\", raw[1])\n\t}\n\n\tvalue, err := strconv.ParseFloat(valueString, 64)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tif strings.EqualFold(valueString, \"nan\") {\n\t\t\tvalue = math.NaN()\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\treturn time.Time{}, 0, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tseconds := int64(tsFloat)\n\tnanos := int64((tsFloat - float64(seconds)) * float64(time.Second))\n\treturn time.Unix(seconds, nanos).UTC(), value, nil\n}\n\ntype promResponse struct {\n\tStatus string `json:\"status\"`\n\tData   struct {\n\t\tResultType string           `json:\"resultType\"`\n\t\tResult     []instantResult  `json:\"result\"`\n\t} `json:\"data\"`\n\tErrorType string `json:\"errorType\"`\n\tError     string `json:\"error\"`\n}\n\ntype promRangeResponse struct {\n\tStatus string `json:\"status\"`\n\tData   struct {\n\t\tResultType string          `json:\"resultType\"`\n\t\tResult     []rangeResult   `json:\"result\"`\n\t} `json:\"data\"`\n\tErrorType string `json:\"errorType\"`\n\tError     string `json:\"error\"`\n}\n\ntype instantResult struct {\n\tMetric map[string]string `json:\"metric\"`\n\tValue  []any             `json:\"value\"`\n}\n\ntype rangeResult struct {\n\tMetric map[string]string `json:\"metric\"`\n\tValues [][]any           `json:\"values\"`\n}\n\n---\npackage kube\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"errors\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"os\"\n\t\"path/filepath\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\t\"time\"\n\n\tcorev1 \"k8s.io/api/core/v1\"\n\tmetav1 \"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1\"\n\t\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/unstructured\"\n\t\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/schema\"\n\t\"k8s.io/client-go/dynamic\"\n\t\"k8s.io/client-go/kubernetes\"\n\t\"k8s.io/client-go/rest\"\n\t\"k8s.io/client-go/tools/clientcmd\"\n\t\"k8s.io/client-go/util/homedir\"\n)\n\ntype Client struct {\n\tclientset *kubernetes.Clientset\n\tdynamic   dynamic.Interface\n}\n\ntype WarningEvent struct {\n\tNamespace string\n\tReason    string\n\tMessage   string\n\tObject    string\n\tWhen      time.Time\n}\n\ntype FluxResource struct {\n\tKind           string\n\tNamespace      string\n\tName           string\n\tReady          bool\n\tSuspended      bool\n\tStatus         string\n\tMessage        string\n\tLastTransition time.Time\n}\n\ntype VolsyncSource struct {\n\tName             string\n\tNamespace        string\n\tSchedule         string\n\tSourcePVC        string\n\tMethod           string\n\tStatus           string\n\tMessage          string\n\tLastResult       string\n\tLastSyncTime     time.Time\n\tNextSyncTime     time.Time\n\tLastSyncDuration       string\n\tStatus         string\n\tMessage        string\n\tLastTransition time.Time\n}\n\nfunc NewClient(kubeconfigPath string) (*Client, error) {\n\tcfg, err := buildConfig(kubeconfigPath)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tclientset, err := kubernetes.NewForConfig(cfg)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"build clientset: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tdyn, err := dynamic.NewForConfig(cfg)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"build dynamic client: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\treturn &Client{\n\t\tclientset: clientset,\n\t\tdynamic:   dyn,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\nfunc (c *Client) WarningEvents(ctx context.Context, limit int) ([]WarningEvent, error) {\n\tif c == nil || c.clientset == nil {\n\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"kubernetes client unavailable\")\n\t}\n\n\tevents, err := c.clientset.CoreV1().Events(\"\").List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tresult := make([]WarningEvent, 0, len(events.Items))\n\tfor _, event := range events.Items {\n\t\tif event.Type != corev1.EventTypeWarning {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\twhen := event.LastTimestamp.Time\n\t\tif when.IsZero() {\n\t\t\twhen = event.EventTime.Time\n\t\t}\n\t\tif when.IsZero() {\n\t\t\twhen = event.CreationTimestamp.Time\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tresult = append(result, WarningEvent{\n\t\t\tNamespace: event.Namespace,\n\t\t\tReason:    event.Reason,\n\t\t\tMessage:   event.Message,\n\t\t\tObject:    fmt.Sprintf(\"%s/%s\", event.InvolvedObject.Kind, event.InvolvedObject.Name),\n\t\t\tWhen:      when,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\tsort.Slice(result, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\treturn result[i].When.After(result[j].When)\n\t})\n\n\tif limit > 0 && len(result) > value,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\treturn samples, nil\n}\n\nfunc (c *Client) QueryRange(ctx context.Context, query string, start, end time.Time, step time.Duration) ([]RangeSeries, error) {\n\tresponse := **Tool Call: Run cat <<'EOF' >/tmp/homelab_bench.sh
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
base=${1:-http://localhost:8080}
endpoints=(
  /healthz
  /api/view/hub
  /api/view/security
  /api/view/anomalies
  /api/view/forecasting
)
for ep in "${endpoints[@]}"; do
  out=()
  for i in $(seq 1 10); do
    line=$(curl -sS -o /dev/null -w '%{http_code} %{time_total}' "$base$ep") || line="000 ERR"
    out+=("$line")
  done
  printf '%s\n' "ENDPOINT $ep"
  printf '%s\n' "${out[@]}"
  printf '%s\n' "---"
done
EOF

## Assistant

The health endpoint is effectively free. The expensive part is in the view APIs, so I’m letting the full benchmark finish before correlating it with browser timings and the handler internals.The three measured JSON views are all landing in the same rough band, about `1.2s` to `2.0s`. That pattern points away from a single page template problem and toward shared request-time data loading in the service layer.

nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tsnapshot, ok := envoyRouteSnapshots[name]\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\trouteNamespace, routeName := parseEnvoyRoute(name)\n\t\t\tsnapshot = &envoyRouteSnapshot{\n\t\t\t\tName:      name,\n\t\t\t\tNamespace: routeNamespace,\n\t\t\t\tRoute:     routeName,\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tenvoyRouteSnapshots[name] = snapshot\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn snapshot\n\t}\n\tensureToolhiveBackendSnapshot := func(name string) *toolhiveBackendSnapshot {\n\t\tname = strings.TrimSpace(name)\n\t\tif name == \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tsnapshot, ok := toolhiveBackendSnapshots[name]\n\t\tif !ok *renovateProjectSnapshot {\n\t\tname = strings.TrimSpace(name)\n\t\tif name == \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tsnapshot, ok := renovateProjectSnapshots[name]\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tsnapshot = &renovateProjectSnapshot{Name: name}\n\t\t\trenovateProjectSnapshots[name] = snapshot\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn snapshot\n\t}\n\n\trecordScalar := func(query string, dest *float64) {\n\t\tvalue, err := s.prom.Scalar(ctx, query)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrors = append(errors, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s: %v\", query, err))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif math.IsNaN(value) {\n\t\t\tvalue = 0\n\t\t}\n\t\t*dest = value\n\t}\n\n\trecordVector := func(query string, apply func([]prom.Sample)) {\n\t\tvalues, err := s.prom.Query(ctx, query)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrors = append(errors, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s: %v\", query, err))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tapply(values)\n\t}\n\n\trecordRange := func(query string, dest *[]float64) {\n\t\tend := time.Now().UTC()\n\t\tstart := end.Add(-24 * time.Hour)\n\t\tseries, err := s.prom.QueryRange(ctx, query, start, end, time.Hour)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrors = append(errors, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s: %v\", query, err))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\t*dest = flattenSeries(series)\n\t}\n\n\trecordScalar(`sum(kube_node_status_condition{condition=\"Ready\",status=\"true\"})`, &data.nodesReady)\n\trecordScalar(`count(kube_node_info)`, func(name string) *toolhiveBackendSnapshot {\n\t\tname = strings.TrimSpace(name)\n\t\tif name == \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tsnapshot, ok := toolhiveBackendSnapshots[name]\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tsnapshot = &toolhiveBackendSnapshot{Name: name}\n\t\t\ttoolhiveBackendSnapshots[name] = snapshot\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn snapshot\n\t}\n\tensureRenovateProjectSnapshot := func(name string) *renovateProjectSnapshot {\n\t\tname = strings.TrimSpace(name)\n\t\tif name == \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tsnapshot, ok := renovateProjectSnapshots[name]\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tsnapshot = &renovateProjectSnapshot{Name: name}\n\t\t\trenovateProjectSnapshots[name] = snapshot\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn snapshot\n\t}\n\n\trecordScalar := func(query string, dest *float64) {\n\t\tvalue, err := s.prom.Scalar(ctx, query)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrors = append(errors, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s: %v\", query, err))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif math.IsNaN(value) {\n\t\t\tvalue = 0\n\t\t}\n\t\t*dest = value\n\t}\n\n\trecordVector := func(query string, apply func([]prom.Sample)) {\n\t\tvalues, err := s.prom.Query(ctx, query)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrors = append(errors, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s: %v\", query, err))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tapply(values)\n\t}\n\n\trecordRange := func(query string, dest *[]float64) {\n\t\tend := time.Now().UTC()\n\t\tstart := end.Add(-24 * time.Hour)\n\t\tseries, err := s.prom.QueryRange(ctx, query, start, end, time.Hour)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrors = append(errors, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s: %v\", query, err))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\t*dest = flattenSeries(series)\n\t}\n\n\trecordScalar(`sum(kube_node_status_condition{condition=\"Ready\",status=\"true\"})`, &data.nodesReady)\n\trecordScalar(`count(kube_node_info)`, \"Ready\"\n\t\t\t\tentry.Tone = \"good\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdata.fluxKinds = append(data.fluxKinds, *entry)\n\t\t}\n\t\tsort.Slice(data.fluxKinds, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn {\n\t\t\tsnapshot = &toolhiveBackendSnapshot{Name: name}\n\t\t\ttoolhiveBackendSnapshots[name] = snapshot\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn snapshot\n\t}\n\tensureRenovateProjectSnapshot := func(name string) *renovateProjectSnapshot {\n\t\tname = strings.TrimSpace(name)\n\t\tif name == \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tsnapshot, ok := renovateProjectSnapshots[name]\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tsnapshot = &renovateProjectSnapshot{Name: name}\n\t\t\trenovateProjectSnapshots[name] = snapshot\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn snapshot\n\t}\n\n\trecordScalar := func(query string, dest *float64) {\n\t\tvalue, err := s.prom.Scalar(ctx, query)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrors = append(errors, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s: %v\", query, err))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif math.IsNaN(value) {\n\t\t\tvalue = 0\n\t\t}\n\t\t*dest = value\n\t}\n\n\trecordVector := func(query string, apply func([]prom.Sample)) {\n\t\tvalues, err := s.prom.Query(ctx, query)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrors = append(errors, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s: %v\", query, err))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tapply(values)\n\t}\n\n\trecordRange := func(query string, dest *[]float64) {\n\t\tend := time.Now().UTC()\n\t\tstart := end.Add(-24 * time.Hour)\n\t\tseries, err := s.prom.QueryRange(ctx, query, start, end, time.Hour)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrors = append(errors, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s: %v\", query, err))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\t*dest = flattenSeries(series)\n\t}\n\n\trecordScalar(`sum(kube_node_status_condition{condition=\"Ready\",status=\"true\"})`, &data.nodesReady)\n\trecordScalar(`count(kube_node_info)`, <script>\n      (function () {\n        const body = document.body;\n        const screen = body.dataset.screen;\n        const refreshSeconds = Number(body.dataset.refreshSeconds || \"45\");\n ## User

No, playwright won't work as it's on the cluster, and you're running the app locally, it won't work

## Assistant

**Findings**
- High: the live slow Envoy route is the dashboard itself, not some other backend. Prometheus shows `httproute/monitor/homelab-dashboard/rule/0` at about `1383.7ms` average over 5m; the next slowest route is about `97.1ms`. That matches the local endpoint timings, so the warning is real and is coming from this app.
- High: every dashboard request rebuilds the full cluster snapshot synchronously. `/api/view/security` goes through [server.go](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/web/server.go:130) -> [Security](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/dashboard/service.go:85) -> [loadShared/collectShared](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/dashboard/service.go:338). In `collectShared`, one request performs `41` scalar Prometheus queries, `40` vector Prometheus queries, `7` range Prometheus queries, and `5` Kubernetes list calls, all in sequence.
- High: the Prometheus client is strictly one HTTP request per query with no batching or fan-out concurrency. [prom/client.go](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/prom/client.go:46) and [prom/client.go](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/prom/client.go:69) both call [do](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/prom/client.go:115) immediately, so the request path is effectively serialized across ~88 Prometheus round trips.
- Medium: the Kubernetes side also does full-cluster list operations on every request. [WarningEvents](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/kube/client.go:104) lists all events cluster-wide, then filters/sorts in memory; [FluxResources](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/kube/client.go:148), [VolsyncSources](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/kube/client.go:200), [ExternalSecrets](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/kube/client.go:252), and [ClusterSecretStores](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/kube/client.go:304) are also called per request from [service.go](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/dashboard/service.go:1154).
- Medium: there is no snapshot cache. The HTML routes and `/api/view/*` routes both recompute the same shared data every time, despite the UI already having a `RefreshSeconds` cadence.

**HTTP Benchmarks**
- `/healthz`: avg `0.3ms`, p95 `0.4ms`, `NEW`
- `/api/view/hub`: avg `1550.7ms`, p95 `1901.4ms`, `NEW`
- `/api/view/security`: avg `1647.5ms`, p95 `2037.0ms`, `NEW`
- `/api/view/anomalies`: avg `1546.2ms`, p95 `1948.5ms`, `NEW`
- `/api/view/forecasting`: avg `1611.5ms`, p95 `1852.9ms`, `NEW`

There is no baseline yet in `registry.md`, so all entries are `NEW`. Playwright was skipped because you’re right: running the app locally cannot reproduce the real cluster/browser path meaningfully.

**Most Likely Culprit**
The main culprit is [collectShared](/Users/movi/Dev/Private/worktrees/homelab-dashboard/smooth-warbler/homelab-dashboard/internal/dashboard/service.go:346). It is doing too much synchronous I/O per request. The similar latency across all four JSON views is the giveaway: the slow part is the shared loader, not page-specific rendering.

**Top 3 Candidates**
1. Synchronous blocking in `collectShared`
```diff
- recordScalar(...)
- recordScalar(...)
- recordVector(...)
- recordRange(...)
+ g, ctx := errgroup.WithContext(ctx)
+ g.Go(func() error { data.nodesReady = queryScalar(ctx, `...`); return nil })
+ g.Go(func() error { data.nodesTotal = queryScalar(ctx, `...`); return nil })
+ g.Go(func() error { topCPU = queryVector(ctx, `...`); return nil })
+ ...
+ _ = g.Wait()
```

2. Missing caching of the shared snapshot
```diff
- func (s *Service) loadShared(ctx context.Context) (sharedData, []string) {
-     return s.collectShared(ctx)
- }
+ func (s *Service) loadShared(ctx context.Context) (sharedData, []string) {
+     if snap, ok := s.cache.GetFresh(30 * time.Second); ok {
+         return snap.data, snap.errors
+     }
+     data, errs := s.collectShared(ctx)
+     s.cache.Store(data, errs)
+     return data, errs
+ }
```

3. Full-cluster Kubernetes listing on every request
```diff
- events, err := c.clientset.CoreV1().Events("").List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
+ events, err := c.clientset.CoreV1().Events(ns).List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{
+     FieldSelector: "type=Warning",
+     Limit: 50,
+ })
```

If you want the shortest path to fixing the warning, I would do them in this order: `1) parallelize Prometheus collection`, `2) add a short TTL cache for shared data`, `3) trim or background the Kubernetes lists`. If you want, I can implement those changes next.
